ASSERTION REASON
A) Both A and R are true and R is the correct explanation of A
B) Both A and R are true but R is not the correct explanation of A
C) A is true but R is false
D) A is false but R is true

1. A: Pyridoxine should be prescribed in pregnant women and malnourished patients taking isoniazid.
R: Pyridoxine reduces risk of neuropathy.

2. A: Rituximab is indicated in RA where response to DMARDs are inadequate. R: Rituximab is an antibody to CD20.

3. A: Isotretinoin is used in the treatment of severe acne. R: Isotretinoin reduces sebum excretion.

4. A: Antivenom is the most important tool in treating envenomation. R: Antivenom binds to venom toxins and renders them inactive.

5. A: All pregnant women who are ART naďve should start ART as soon as possible. R: ART reduces the risk of mother-to-child transmission of HIV to 0.01%.

6. A: SSRIs are first-line treatment for major depressive disorder. R: SSRIs increase dopamine levels by inhibiting its reuptake.

7. A: Organophosphate poisoning causes miosis and bradycardia.
  R: Organophosphates inhibit acetylcholinesterase, leading to excessive acetylcholine at synapses.

8. A: SLE primarily affects older adults.
  R: SLE is caused by autosomal dominant mutation with excessive neutrophil activation.

9. A: In lepromatous leprosy, the lepromin skin test is usually negative.
R: Lepromatous leprosy is characterized by strong cell-mediated immunity against
M. leprae.

10. A: Mycobacterium tuberculosis spreads hematogenously.
R: It causes granulomatous inflammation at the base of the brain.











A) Both A and R are true and R is the correct explanation of A
B) Both A and R are true but R is not the correct explanation of A
C) A is true but R is false
D) A is false but R is true

11. A: Acute cholinergic syndrome starts within minutes of exposure and presents with nicotinic or muscarinic features.
R: Early atropine use is potentially lifesaving.

12. A: Accumulation of serous fluid in the peritoneal space is called pericardial effusion.
  R: Pleural fluid accumulates due to increased hydrostatic/decreased oncotic pressure.

13. A: Hematopoiesis is impaired in HIV.
R: HIV affects hematopoiesis directly or via cytokines.

14. A: DMARDs are small molecule immune response inhibitors.
R: They do not cause marrow/liver toxicity and need no regular monitoring.

15. A: Secondary syphilis occurs 6-8 weeks after chancre. R: Treponemes disseminate causing multisystem disease.

16. A: SSRIs are probably the antidepressants of first choice.
R: SSRIs reduce quality of life and have high cardiac side effects.

17. A: Osteoarthritis is the most common form of arthritis. R: Osteoarthritis is strongly associated with ageing.

18. A: First MTP joint is the most commonly affected in gout.
R: First MTP joint is warmer, favoring uric acid crystallization.

19. A: Molluscum contagiosum is caused by a DNA poxvirus. R: It is commonly seen in immunocompromised patients.

20. A: Heliotrope rash is a feature of SLE.
R: Rash in SLE is commonly precipitated by UV light.











A) Both A and R are true and R is the correct explanation of A
B) Both A and R are true but R is not the correct explanation of A
C) A is true but R is false
D) A is false but R is true

21. A: For diagnosing pulmonary embolism, V/Q scan is better than CTPA. R: V/Q scan is more specific than CTPA.

22. A: Seborrhoeic dermatitis is caused by Malassezia yeast.
R: Malassezia triggers complement activation and diminished T-cell response.

23. A: Schizophrenia is commonly seen in families with cortical abnormalities. R: Studies show a role of genetics, mutation, and development.

24. A: Alpha-1 antitrypsin deficiency causes liver cirrhosis and COPD. R: Abnormal AAT accumulates and damages liver and lung tissue.

25. A: Raynaud's phenomenon causes bluish discoloration of fingers in cold. R: Cold causes vasodilation.

26. A: Methotrexate is used in treatment of RA. R: Methotrexate is an anti-inflammatory agent.

27. A: Beta blockers are contraindicated in asthma.
R: Beta blockers cause bronchoconstriction by blocking beta-2 receptors.

28. A: Vitamin B12 deficiency causes megaloblastic anemia. R: B12 deficiency impairs DNA synthesis in RBCs.

29. A: Prolonged PPI use can cause hypomagnesemia.
R: PPI inhibit gastric acid secretion, reducing Mg absorption.

30. A: ARDS causes hypoxemia despite oxygen therapy.
R: ARDS damages alveolar-capillary membrane, impairing O2 diffusion.











A) Both statements are correct and R explains A
B) Both correct, but R does not explain A
C) A is correct but R is incorrect
D) A is incorrect but R is correct
E) Both are incorrect

31. A: Sacroiliitis is a hallmark of ankylosing spondylitis.
R: It occurs due to immune complex deposition in SI joints.

32. A: Benzodiazepines should be avoided in CLD.
R: They are metabolized in liver and can precipitate encephalopathy.

33. A: Folinic acid must always be given with high-dose methotrexate.
R: Folinic acid inhibits dihydrofolate reductase to counter methotrexate.

34. A: Oximes are not recommended in carbamate poisoning.
R: Carbamates cause irreversible acetylcholinesterase inhibition.

35. A: Empirical antibiotics should be delayed until LP in suspected meningitis. R: Giving antibiotics before LP sterilizes CSF, affecting diagnosis.

36. A: Enfuvirtide is an integrase inhibitor used in Hepatitis C. R: Enfuvirtide acts via antagonizing CCR5 antigen.

37. A: Acute gout patient can have normal serum uric acid. R: Febuxostat is used to reduce uric acid levels.

38. A: Compression of right upper lobe bronchus by mass causes absorption collapse.
R: Golden S sign is a radiological feature of right upper lobe collapse.

39. A: Acute rheumatic fever causes migratory arthritis. R: Joint involvement is erosive and deforming.

40. A: ALT/AST values are >1000 IU in viral hepatitis A.
R: PT/INR is used to monitor severity of illness in hepatitis.











A) A and R are true; R explains A
B) A and R are true; R does not explain A
C) A is true; R is false
D) A is false; R is true

41. A: EDH is usually due to rupture of middle meningeal artery. R: Epidural hematomas often show lucid interval post trauma.

42. A: Recurrent laryngeal nerve injury is a serious complication of thyroidectomy. R: It lies close to inferior thyroid artery and may be damaged.

43. A: Varicose veins are more common in lower limbs.
R: Prolonged standing increases venous pressure, causing valve incompetence.

44. A: MEN 2A is associated with pheochromocytoma, MTC, and hyperparathyroidism.
R: RET proto-oncogene mutation is responsible.

45. A: Buerger's disease is strongly associated with tobacco use.
R: Tobacco causes endothelial damage and thrombosis in small/medium arteries.

46. A: Cefotaxime is not the drug of choice for mycoplasma pneumonia.
R: Mycoplasma lacks cell wall and cefotaxime inhibits cell wall synthesis.

47. A: ART is recommended for all HIV patients regardless of CD4 count. R: It reduces HIV-related morbidity and mortality.

48. A: Prednisolone for alcoholic hepatitis can be started if SOFA >2.
R: SOFA >2 indicates sepsis, and glucocorticoids are avoided in sepsis.

49. A: ACE inhibitors and beta-blockers are used in EF <40%. R: They are first-line in CCF with reduced EF.

50. A: Sacubitril/valsartan is preferred in symptomatic chronic heart failure.
  R: Mineralocorticoid receptor antagonists are first-line in heart failure with reduced EF













A) Both A and R are true and R is the correct explanation of A
B) Both A and R are true but R is not the correct explanation of A
C) A is true but R is false
D) A is false but R is true
E) Both A and B are correct

51. A: 45-year-old male with chronic cough, night sweats, and hemoptysis should be evaluated with sputum microscopy and GeneXpert.
  R: Mycobacterium tuberculosis primarily affects lungs and these tests provide microbiological confirmation.

52. A: A 62-year-old COPD patient with polycythemia should be evaluated for secondary erythrocytosis.
R: Chronic hypoxia stimulates erythropoietin production leading to polycythemia.

53. A: 58-year-old male with recurrent thrombosis and plethoric complexion has polycythemia vera.
  R: Polycythemia vera is caused by chronic hypoxia increasing erythropoietin levels.

54. A: 35-year-old female with weight loss, heat intolerance, palpitations, and exophthalmos likely has Graves' disease.
R: Hyperthyroidism in Graves' disease is caused by excessive iodine intake.

55. A: 60-year-old male with COVID-19 and hypoxia should receive supportive care and oxygen.
  R: COVID-19 primarily causes bacterial pneumonia needing broad-spectrum antibiotics
56. A: BP should not be lowered in ischemic stroke unless >220/120 mm Hg. R: Lowering BP increases size of ischemic penumbra.

57. A: Acute pulmonary embolism is an example of hypovolemic shock. R: DVT is a risk factor for pulmonary embolism.


58. A: Cryptococcal meningitis is an opportunistic infection in HIV. R: Risk is high when CD4 <100 cells/mmł.

59. A: Gout is a crystal-induced arthritis.
R: Urate-lowering therapy is immediately started once diagnosed.

60. A: Severe hypothermia is defined as core temp <28°C. R: Old age is the highest risk factor for hypothermia.



A) A and R are true and R is the correct explanation of A
B) A and R are true but R is not the correct explanation of A
C) A is true but R is false
D) A is false but R is true

61. A: SSRIs are commonly prescribed for depression.
R: SSRIs increase serotonin by inhibiting reuptake and relieve symptoms.

62. A: Antibiotic resistance is a growing concern in treating infections. R: Resistance leads to failure and spread of resistant strains.

63. A: Vitamin B12 deficiency leads to megaloblastic anemia. R: B12 is essential for DNA synthesis in RBCs.

64. A: Corticosteroids are used in chronic asthma.
R: They reduce airway inflammation and prevent exacerbations.

65. A: TSH levels are used to diagnose hypothyroidism.
R: TSH increases in hypothyroidism to stimulate underactive thyroid.

19. 
Select the correct statement regarding types of debridement:
i. Surgical - Excision of non-viable tissue using surgical instruments such as a scalpel, curette, or scissors until healthy bleeding occurs at the wound edges
ii. Enzymatic - Chemically liquefy necrotic tissue with enzymes using topical agents such as collagenase or papain-urea
iii. Autolytic - Using dressings such as hydrocolloids or transparent films to retain moisture and allow wound enzymes to selectively liquefy non-viable tissue
iv. Mechanical - Non-selective debridement such as using irrigation, wet-to-dry dressings, and hydrotherapy. Both non-viable and viable tissue may be removed
v. Biological - Medical-grade larvae of Lucilia sericata release proteolytic and antimicrobial substances to remove necrotic tissue

Options:
A. i, iii, v
B. ii, iv
C. i, ii, iii, iv, v
D. iii, iv, v

SURGERY
Assertion and reason type
a. Both Assertion and Reasoning are true, and the reasoning is a correct explanation of the assertion.
 b. Both Assertion and Reasoning are true, but the reasoning is NOT a correct explanation of the assertion.
c. Assertion is true, but the Reasoning is false.
 d. Assertion is false, but the Reasoning is true, but not applicable as A by itself is false
1. 
Assertion: Around a quarter of acute appendicitis treated successfully with antibiotics needs surgery for recurrent symptoms in a year.
Reasoning: Antibiotics work successfully in up to 90% of uncomplicated acute appendicitis.


2. 
Assertion: Eradication of H. pylori with medication can be achieved in 90% of patients with peptic ulcer and should be instituted.
Reasoning: H. pylori is crucial in the development of peptic ulcer.



3. 
Assertion: Pilonidal sinus cases with minimal symptoms may be treated with cleaning, hygiene and shaving hair frequently.
Reasoning: Natural history of pilonidal disease is usually one of regression.



4. 
Assertion: A mesenteric cyst moves freely from the right lower quadrant to left upper quadrant.
Reasoning: The root of mesentery spans from the right sacroiliac joint to the left second lumbar transverse process.





5. 
Assertion: Radical excision is the treatment of choice for choledochal cysts. Reasoning: Excision of the cyst reduces the rate of recurrent cholangitis and malignancy.
6. 
Assertion: Insulin resistance in postoperative patients is primarily caused by increased glucose production.
Reason: Decreased glucose uptake in peripheral tissues contributes significantly to insulin resistance.


7. 
Assertion: Muscle wasting during the catabolic phase involves activation of the ubiquitin-proteasome pathway.
Reason: This pathway primarily enhances muscle protein synthesis.



8. 
Assertion (A): Blood transfusions should be given to achieve a haemoglobin level of
>10 g/dL in all patients.
Reason (R): Achieving a haemoglobin level of >10 g/dL has been shown to be unnecessary and associated with increased morbidity and mortality compared to lower target values.


9. 
Assertion (A): Shaving immediately before surgery reduces the risk of surgical site infections (SSIs) compared to shaving the night before.
Reason (R): Shaving the night before surgery can lead to minor skin injury that enhances superficial bacterial colonization, thereby increasing the risk of SSIs.


10. 
Assertion (A): Keloid scars extend beyond the boundaries of the original incision or wound and do not spontaneously regress.
Reason (R): Keloid scars contain excess collagen, which is arranged in a disorganized pattern

Reasoning: Antibiotics work successfully in up to 90% of uncomplicated acute appendicitis.

Reason: Common bile duct injury is a serious complication of cholecystectomy.

Reason: CEA is a highly specific and sensitive tumor marker.

(TVS)

Spiegelberg criteria

Decidual reaction


66.a) Diagnosis:
Surgical Site Infection (SSI) - likely deep incisional type.

b) Causative organisms:


? Escherichia coli

? Bacteroides fragilis

? Staphylococcus aureus

? Streptococcus spp. (± MRSA, Pseudomonas in hospital-acquired cases)


c) Abnormality in blood investigation:

? Leukocytosis (? WBC count)

? ? CRP, ± positive wound culture


d) Surgical treatment:

? Open wound at suture site

? Drain pus, irrigate, debride if needed

? Leave wound open for secondary healing

? Start empirical antibiotics


e) Prevention:

? Pre-op antibiotic prophylaxis

? Aseptic surgical technique

? Proper wound care post-op

? Good glycemic control and minimal tissue trauma

11. Regarding sheehan's syndrome

12. Regarding puerperium

2. Lochia immediately following delivery is called lochia Alba.

3. Puerperal pyrexia is defined as temperature elevation occurring on 2 or more occasions within 24hrs postpartum.
4. Postpartum blues require pharmacotherapy with antidepressants.

b. 1,3 & 4 are false

c. 2, 3 & 4 are false

d. 1, 2 & 4 are false

9. Assertion-In normal pregnancy a woman needs about 9 mg of iron

MCQ - Multiple Correct Answers Type
1. Regarding Vitamin D deficiency in children:
I. Earliest radiological sign is a generalised reduction in bone density
II. Breast milk is a poor source of vitamin D
III. Stoss therapy is the currently recommended therapy
IV. Parathyroid hormone levels are high in nutritional vitamin D deficiency
a. All are false statements
b. Only I & III are true
c. Only II & IV are true
d. Only IV is true
2. Regarding Sickle Cell Disease:
I. Patients who are homozygous for HbS have sickle cell trait
II. Hydroxyurea is used to increase the production of HbF
III. Immunization with pneumococcal vaccine is recommended
IV. Splenomegaly is a common finding in older children
a. I, II, III are true
b. Only II & III are true
c. II, III & IV are true
d. Only I & IV are true

IV. Erythema marginatum

c. I, II, III, IV
d. I, III & IV

b. Only I, II & III are true
c. Only II, III, IV are true
d. Only III & IV are true

ASSERTION AND REASONING TYPE QUESTIONS



General instructions
A) Both A and R are true, and R is the correct explanation for A.
B) Both A and R are true, but R is not the correct explanation for A.
C) A is true, but R is false
D) A is false, but R is true.


1. Assertion (A): Wilms Tumor is associated with aniridia (absence of the iris).

Reason (R): This is due to a genetic mutation affecting the WTI gene.


2. Assertion (A): Children with fat malabsorption states are predisposed to vitamin A deficiency
Reason (R): Fat malabsorption leads to malabsorption of fat soluble vitamins.


3. Assertion (A): Therapy with primaquine is indicated in vivax malaria
Reason (R): Primaquine prevents the elimination of the exoerythrocytic stages in the liver

4. Assertion (A). Children develop fine motor skills before gross motor skills Reason (R).Motor development follows a cephalocaudal and proximodistal pattern
5. A:Short stature on children can be a sign of an underlying medical condition R:Growth hormone deficiency is the most common cause of short stature in children.

6. A:Stridor is a danger sign
R: Stridor Indicates upper airway obstruction
7. A Excess cow's Milk ingestion predisposes to iron deficiency anemia B Calcium in cow's milk inhibits iron absorption









8. Assertion (A): An autosomal dominant genetic disease affecting one parent gives a 50% chance of inheritance in offspring.
Reason (R): Autosomal dominant alleles can cause disease in heterozygous states.



9. Assertion (A): Deworming is not recommended for infants below 6 months. Reason (R): Bile salt stimulated lipase in breast milk kills intestinal parasites.



10. Assertion (A): Children with Down syndrome require routine screening for congenital hypothyroidism.
Reason (R): Trisomy 21 increases the risk of autoimmune thyroiditis.



 11. Assertion (A): Managing childhood-onset diabetes requires insulin at regular intervals.
Reason (R): Insulin resistance is the primary defect in type 1 diabetes.



12. Assertion (A): Iron deficiency anemia is a significant risk factor for poor school performance in children.
Reason (R): Iron deficiency primarily affects physical strength without impacting cognitive function.
























A. Both A and R are true, and R is the correct explanation for A.
B. Both A and R are true, but R is not the correct explanation for A.
C. A is true, but R is false
D. A is false, but R is true.


13. Assertion: Breast feeding during night should be encouraged Reason: Oxytocin secretion is increased in a relaxed mother
14) Assertion: In nephrotic syndrome, 2 consecutive relapses while on alternate day steroids is steroid dependance
Reason:.High dose steroid is the treatment of choice for steroid dependent

15. Assertion: Routine administration of prophylactic vitamin k is recommended at birth to all healthy newborns.
Reason: Newborns don't have adequate intestinal bacterial flora for synthesizing vitamin K
16. Assertion: During measles outbreak measles vaccine cannot be given to infants less than 9 months
Reason: According to the national immunization schedule MMR vaccine is given at 9-12 months and 16-24 months.
17. Assertion :WHO ORS contain glucose and sodium in 1:1 ratio.
Reason: WHO ORS uses the principle of glucose independent sodium and water absorption.

18. Assertion: Absence of wheezing in the presence of cyanosis and respiratory distress in asthma should not be considered as evidence of clinical improvement.
Reason: Mucous plug occluding the bronchi may cause collapse of small segments of lung.







19. Assertion:Down syndrome children are advised not to participate in contact sports.

Reason In 10-30% cases of down syndrome reported to have atlanto-occipital subluxation.
20. Assertion (A): Short stature in children is always indicative of a serious underlying health condition.
Reasoning (R): Short stature can sometimes be a normal variant in children, such as in familial short stature or constitutional delay of growth and puberty.


20. Assertion (A): If a neonate is not breathing and has a heart rate above 100 beats per minute, positive pressure ventilation should still be provided.

Reasoning (R): Positive pressure ventilation is required to ensure that the neonate's lungs expand and provide oxygenation, even if the heart rate is above 100 beats per minute.

21. Assertion (A): Henoch-Schönlein Purpura is associated with glomerulonephritis in a significant number of cases.
Reasoning (R): HSP can cause renal involvement, leading to glomerulonephritis, which manifests as hematuria or proteinuria in some patients.

22,Assertion (A): Hyponatremia can occur due to excessive water intake, diluting the sodium concentration in the blood.

Reasoning (R): Hyponatremia can also result from sodium loss through excessive sweating( cystic fibrosis) or diarrhea, leading to decreased sodium levels.

 23.(A): Main treatment for Breath Holding spell is iron supplementation (R): Breath Holding spell is a type of seizure.








A. Both A and R are true, and R is the correct explanation for A.
B. Both A and R are true, but R is not the correct explanation for A.
C. A is true, but R is false
D. A is false, but R is true.




24.(A): Glucose is one of the main constituents of ORS

(R): Glucose helps to correct dehydration and electrolyte abnormalities

25.(A): Iron deficiency anemia is macrocytic anemia.

(R): Macrocytic anemia is due to decreased DNA synthesis.

26.(A): Vit K is given to all newborns at birth
(R) Hepatitis B vaccine is given to all newborns at birth

27. Assertion: Gastric lavage is contraindicated in hydrocarbon pneumonia. Reason-It can lead to perforation

28. Assertion: Consumption of goat milk can cause megaloblastic anemia. Reason: as goat milk is deficient in zinc.

29. Assertion- Celiac disease is triggered by ingestion of wheat gluten.

Reason- Most common extra intestinal manifestation in celiac disease is iron deficiency anemia.


30. Assertion -Type 1 diabetes mellitus is a chronic condition in which pancreas produce little or no insulin
Reasoning-It is caused by genes and environmental factors such as viruses which destroy insulin producing beta cells of pancreas (autoimmune condition).









31. Assertion - Adding malted food increases energy density Reason - Amylase rich food increases the viscosity and bulk of food

32. Assertion (A) - Ivig is used in the treatment of ITP.
Reason(R)-In ITP, there is immune mediated platelet destruction.

33. A): Bone age is less than the chronological age in constitutional delay of growth and puberty

(R): IgF1 levels tend to be low for chronological age but normal for bone age in these patients.


34. Assertion (A) - Developmental surveillance must be done in a routine manner.
Reason(R)-Child development is a dynamic process and is difficult to quantify by one time assessment.


35. Assertion (A) - In AGN, hypertensive encephalopathy is one of the complications.

Reason(R)-In AGN, there is a decreased colloid osmotic pressure.

 36. Assertion (A) - Respiratory distress syndrome is common in a preterm born to IDM.
Reason(R)-Infants of diabetic mothers are macrosomic.


37. Assertion (A)-k" is the most abundant action of ECF.
Reason(R)-Hyperkalemia can be associated with flat T wave and shortened

B. Both A and R are true, but R is not the correct explanation for A.
C. A is true, but R is false
D. A is false, but R is true.


38. Assertion: Breast milk has anti-infective effect Reason: Breast milk is rich in IgE and lactoferrin

 39. Assertion: Cardiogenic shock is the most common cause of shock in the pediatric age group.
Reason: Hypotension is an early sign and seen in compensated shock


40. Assertion: Malaria fever appears at the merozoite stage of Plasmodium. Reason: The infective stage of Plasmodium is sporozoite.


41. Assertion-Gingival hypertrophy and bleeding are symptoms of scurvy. Reason-Lack of fresh fruits and vegetables in diet causes scurvy

 45. A .Severe dengue is characterized by severe plasma leakage and severe organ impairment
R. In severe dengue there is respiratory distress and increased liver transaminases
